# Woof Remediation Checkpoint - 2026-06-08

## Completed in this pass

- Added production app-config validation for Supabase, Google OAuth, and RevenueCat keys.
- Added `scripts/validate-config.js` and package scripts for config and dependency audit checks.
- Declared `expo-constants` as a direct dependency.
- Aligned Expo SDK 55 package patches with `expo install --fix`.
- Removed RevenueCat placeholder API-key fallbacks.
- Changed RevenueCat initialization to track the configured app user and switch identity after sign-in.
- Changed entitlement checks to return an unknown state on transient RevenueCat failures instead of forcing `false`.
- Stopped client-side writes of user OCR data into the shared `product_data` catalog.
- Replaced direct user OCR catalog ingestion with a trusted Edge-owned path:
  - OCR recovery sends `user_ocr` provenance and parsed ingredients inside the verified analysis request,
  - mobile code still skips direct `user_ocr` writes to shared `product_data`,
  - the `analyze` Edge Function sanitizes OCR catalog payloads and saves through the service-role-only `save_product_data` RPC only after the completed analysis validates,
  - low-quality OCR payloads with missing product names, short ingredient text, implausible ingredient strings, or fewer than 5 parsed ingredients are not saved,
  - the existing RPC merge policy still prevents user OCR from overwriting higher-trust OPFF/scraped product rows,
  - user OCR ingestion guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Added `supabase/migrations/023_security_hardening.sql` to:
  - pin `SECURITY DEFINER` search paths,
  - restrict quota RPCs to the caller or `service_role`,
  - remove public execution from internal rate-limit, cleanup, and catalog-write RPCs,
  - restrict profile updates away from entitlement/quota columns,
  - clamp and freshen `search_products` results.
- Hardened `analyze` and `product-lookup` Edge Functions with request-size checks and fail-closed rate-limit behavior.
- Added bounded quota reconciliation in `services/auth.js`:
  - malformed or oversized local quota mirrors are clamped,
  - guest-to-account carryover can no longer replay unbounded RPC loops,
  - startup waits for local quota hydration before clearing auth loading,
  - sign-out rehydrates guest quota instead of resetting scan count to zero,
  - dev reset helpers no longer write quota columns from the client.
- Changed authenticated `analyze` quota checks to repair a missing `profiles` row under the service role before enforcing quota, and to fail closed when profile lookup or repair fails.
- Added source-level quota guard tests:
  - `npm run test:auth-quota`
  - `npm run test:edge-quota`
  - `npm run test:guards`
- Removed local-script secret fallbacks:
  - scrubbed hardcoded OpenAI-style keys, ScrapingBee fallback keys, Supabase JWT-style keys, and concrete Supabase project URLs from ops/test scripts under `scripts/`,
  - replaced those values with required environment variables,
  - added a source-level secret hygiene guard over `scripts/`,
  - any real values that existed in local scripts should still be rotated outside the repo.
- Fixed Results quota-error conversion routing:
  - quota errors now pass an explicit `onUpgrade` handler to `ErrorState`,
  - the "Upgrade to Pro" CTA now opens Paywall with `source: "quota_error"` instead of routing home.
- Fixed Results route-param crash risk:
  - Results now reads `route.params || {}` before destructuring,
  - malformed or missing navigation params no longer crash before Results can render its own error handling,
  - Results error guard enforces defensive route-param handling.
- Fixed first-scan education toast:
  - `FirstScanToast` is now mounted in the Results success layout,
  - the `@woof_first_scan_toast_shown` flag is written only after the toast becomes visible.
- Added `npm run check:edge` using `deno-bin` and fixed Edge Function type errors so both Supabase functions pass Deno type-checking.
- Generated `deno.lock`, which pins the current remote `esm.sh` Supabase import resolution used by the Edge Function type-check.
- Fixed post-scan upsell timing:
  - quota increment helpers now return the committed count,
  - Results awaits the pet-food scan increment and shows the post-scan prompt from the committed count instead of stale `remainingScans()` timing.
- Fixed text-only human-food retry:
  - retry now preserves `foodName` and `petType`,
  - photo human-food retry also preserves `foodName` when present.
- Fixed Home search race handling:
  - short/cleared queries now invalidate outstanding search responses,
  - stale responses are dropped by sequence and latest-query checks,
  - old rows are cleared as soon as a new valid search starts,
  - result rows render only for a non-loading query of at least 2 characters.
- Fixed Home search error visibility:
  - Supabase RPC search failures now show a visible product-search error card instead of an empty-looking result area,
  - search errors clear on new searches, cleared searches, and successful responses,
  - the error card includes a retry action that reruns the current query,
  - Home search guard covers the visible error and retry path.
- Wired Supabase-backed failures into the offline detector:
  - Home search reports Supabase RPC network failures and successful search round trips,
  - Home history timeout/failure paths report into the global network state,
  - product-data lookup, analysis-cache prewarm/lookup, and cache hit-count paths report network failures and successes,
  - signed-in history read, image enrichment, migration, upsert, and clear calls report Supabase network failures and successes,
  - network reporting guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed search catalog-miss recovery:
  - `classifyError` now has a non-retryable `product_not_found` kind with `action: "scan_product"`,
  - `ErrorState` shows a "Scan Product" CTA for catalog misses,
  - failed search Results screens replace themselves with the Scanner route instead of retrying the same invalid row,
  - recent-search persistence is centralized in `services/recentSearches.js`,
  - rejected search catalog-miss cache keys are removed from recent searches as soon as Results receives the typed product-not-found error,
  - Home rehydrates recent searches on focus so stale rejected rows do not reappear after navigating back,
  - search recovery guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Tightened config and dependency hygiene:
  - `dotenv` is quiet in app config and validation so Expo tooling gets clean output,
  - RevenueCat production validation is platform-aware (`EAS_BUILD_PLATFORM=ios` requires only the iOS key; Android requires only the Android key; unknown production requires both),
  - Expo SDK 55 manifest ranges are aligned with the resolved patch versions,
  - npm overrides `uuid` to `^11.1.1` to clear the transitive Expo `xcode` advisory without changing Expo SDK.
- Updated dependency override hygiene:
  - npm now overrides `shell-quote` to `^1.8.4` to clear the transitive `react-native`/`react-devtools-core` critical advisory,
  - `package-lock.json` resolves `shell-quote` to `1.8.4`.
- Fixed scanner capture cancellation and back navigation:
  - capture is disabled until `CameraView.onCameraReady` fires,
  - camera readiness resets when the scanner loses focus,
  - capture work is tied to a mounted/cancelled session id,
  - cancellation is checked after native capture and again before pushing Results,
  - back during capture now cancels the active session before leaving,
  - the processing Cancel card renders outside the touch-disabled scan-frame overlay,
  - the scanner cancellation guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed camera capture orientation risk:
  - package-photo capture no longer uses `skipProcessing: true`, so Expo can normalize device orientation before vision analysis,
  - ingredient-label capture no longer skips processing before OCR,
  - scanner capture guard enforces orientation-safe capture settings for both camera flows.
- Fixed ingredient-label recovery route validation:
  - IngredientCapture now requires the original product name and front-photo base64 before allowing capture or skip,
  - missing recovery context renders a scan-again state instead of forwarding undefined images into analysis,
  - capture and skip actions expose accessible disabled states when context is invalid,
  - ingredient capture guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed truncated streamed-analysis completion:
  - Claude streaming now rejects incomplete final objects before final `onUpdate`,
  - incomplete streams can use the existing retry/non-streaming fallback path,
  - `analysisService` validates completed pet-food and human-food shapes before marking state complete,
  - local result writes, history writes, and local cache reads reject malformed completed analyses,
  - the analysis-completion guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed scan helper timeout budgets around auth headers:
  - Claude auth-header acquisition is now abort-aware for both `getSession()` and token refresh,
  - streaming, identify, OCR, ingredient lookup, product lookup, and non-streaming analysis deadlines now include auth/session/header work instead of starting only after it,
  - parent cancellation is chained into the same helper request controller,
  - timeout cleanup runs even when auth-header acquisition aborts,
  - app-owned helper deadlines now convert timeout aborts into typed `TimeoutError`/`REQUEST_TIMEOUT` paths instead of looking like user cancellation,
  - Claude timeout guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed expired-session analysis downgrade and recovery:
  - Claude auth-header acquisition now throws a typed `AUTH_SESSION_EXPIRED`/`AuthSessionError` when session lookup fails, token refresh fails, or a signed-in session has no usable access token,
  - refresh/token failures sign out stale local auth state but no longer return anonymous guest headers,
  - explicit no-session guest mode still uses guest headers,
  - OCR and ingredient-lookup helper fallbacks rethrow auth recovery errors instead of swallowing them as label/read/catalog misses,
  - Results passes a `Sign In Again` handler into `ErrorState`; auth errors now clear stale auth and open the Auth modal while preserving the current Results screen for retry,
  - Claude auth-session guard and Results error guard are included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed split SSE streaming parser handling:
  - Claude streaming now buffers incomplete SSE records across `ReadableStream` chunks instead of parsing each chunk as complete lines,
  - events are parsed only after a complete SSE record delimiter arrives, with a final EOF flush for complete trailing records,
  - the full-text SSE fallback uses the same parser as the streaming path,
  - the Claude streaming guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed Paywall in-flight purchase/restore handling:
  - the close button is disabled while purchase or restore is running,
  - dismiss is a no-op during in-flight transactions,
  - purchase and restore callbacks check mounted state after async boundaries,
  - navigation uses a dismissed/mounted `safeGoBack` helper,
  - loading state resets only while the Paywall is still mounted,
  - the Paywall in-flight guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed Pro share-card FileSystem compatibility:
  - Results share-card image handling now uses Expo SDK 55's supported `File`/`Paths` API instead of main-export legacy `cacheDirectory`, `copyAsync`, and `deleteAsync` calls that throw,
  - captured share images are copied into cache with `File.copy()` and cleaned up with `File.delete()`,
  - image-share fallback now shows a user-visible "Shared as Text" alert instead of silently downgrading,
  - share filesystem guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed purchase-completed/no-entitlement handling:
  - RevenueCat purchase and restore checks now use a shared expected Pro entitlement id,
  - completed purchases without active Pro return a typed `no_entitlement` result instead of silently resetting the CTA,
  - diagnostic metadata includes package id, product id, expected entitlement id, active entitlement ids, and all entitlement ids,
  - Paywall shows a "Purchase Received" state with restore and support guidance,
  - restore no-entitlement states also surface support guidance,
  - purchase entitlement guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed RevenueCat identity cleanup:
  - added `logOutPurchases()` to call `Purchases.logOut()` for configured signed-in RevenueCat users and always reset local purchase identity state,
  - Supabase sign-out, auth `SIGNED_OUT` handling, and account deletion now clear RevenueCat identity instead of only resetting a local flag,
  - purchase entitlement guard now covers RevenueCat logout wiring.
- Fixed Profile account-deletion loading state:
  - the destructive delete flow now resets `deleting` and the confirmation-flow lock in a `finally` block after both successful and failed account deletion,
  - same-screen re-authentication can no longer inherit a stale disabled Delete Account button after successful deletion,
  - profile delete guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened account-deletion local data cleanup:
  - added `clearLocalUserData()` to remove scan quota mirrors, human-food quota mirrors, recent searches, local result-cache indexes and payloads, local scan-history rows, history migration flags, and OPFF lookup cache entries,
  - account deletion now clears local disk data and in-memory analysis/history/warm-cache surfaces before calling the server-side account delete RPC, so cleanup failures fail closed while the account still has a retry path,
  - analysis cleanup now aborts in-flight analyses and clears scheduled cleanup timers instead of leaving completed/running scan state in memory after deletion,
  - account-deletion cleanup guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened subscription management support from Profile:
  - paid users now go through an awaited `canOpenURL`/`openURL` subscription-management path,
  - iOS and Android store subscription URLs have platform-specific manual fallback instructions,
  - failed or unsupported store links show support guidance with a support email action,
  - the subscription row has an accessibility hint for both manage and upgrade states,
  - manage subscription guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed hardcoded paywall trial and pricing claims:
  - local plan constants no longer claim every package has a trial,
  - trial CTA, accessibility label, timeline, and trust copy now render only when RevenueCat `introPrice` metadata exposes a free introductory period,
  - annual monthly equivalent uses RevenueCat `pricePerMonthString` or derives from localized price/currency metadata,
  - non-trial trust copy uses the selected package price and subscription period instead of a hardcoded monthly fallback,
  - paywall trial metadata guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed guest human-food quota wording mismatch:
  - guest copy no longer promises a calendar-day reset for a server-side rolling cooldown,
  - signed-in free users still see UTC-day reset copy,
  - anonymous edge quota errors no longer say "daily" for the guest IP cap,
  - guest human-food quota responses still classify as quota errors,
  - the human-food quota guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Verified and guarded dev-only quota reset helpers:
  - `resetScanCount` and `resetHumanFoodQuota` explicitly no-op outside `DEV_MODE`,
  - client code still has no direct profile quota/entitlement column updates,
  - auth quota guards now enforce the dev-helper production no-op invariant.
- Fixed root crash recovery colors:
  - ErrorBoundary fallback no longer references missing `Colors.bg`,
  - recovery screen uses `Colors.background` and `Colors.buttonText`,
  - root recovery guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed onboarding completion regressions:
  - root crash recovery no longer removes `@woof_onboarding_complete`,
  - Profile's "Replay App Intro" now shows onboarding without mutating completed-onboarding storage,
  - skip and final onboarding completion still persist the completed flag,
  - onboarding state guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Narrowed launch platform scope:
  - iOS `supportsTablet` is now false for the phone-first launch until an iPad/tablet QA pass is documented,
  - portrait-only orientation remains guarded,
  - platform scope guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Aligned native appearance with in-app appearance controls:
  - Expo `userInterfaceStyle` is now `automatic` because Profile exposes Auto/Light/Dark and the theme provider resolves against `useColorScheme()`,
  - platform scope guard now enforces that native appearance remains automatic while Auto/Dark controls are present.
- Fixed release metadata mismatches:
  - Expo native display name is now `Woof`, matching the public brand capitalization,
  - `package.json`, `package-lock.json`, and Expo app version are aligned at `1.1.1`,
  - platform scope guard now covers brand capitalization and package/Expo version alignment.
- Fixed camera permission scope copy:
  - iOS `NSCameraUsageDescription` now covers pet food packages, ingredient labels, and human foods,
  - Expo camera plugin permission copy now covers pet food packages, ingredient labels, and human foods,
  - Scanner permission fallback copy now matches the native camera permission scope,
  - platform scope guard now enforces the camera permission wording.
- Added Apple Sign-In runtime availability gating:
  - AuthScreen checks `AppleAuthentication.isAvailableAsync()` and only renders Apple sign-in when supported,
  - `signInWithApple()` checks availability before launching native Apple auth and throws `APPLE_SIGN_IN_UNAVAILABLE`,
  - unavailable Apple auth shows a Google fallback message,
  - Apple auth guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened native Google OAuth:
  - Supabase auth now uses `flowType: "pkce"` while keeping React Native URL auto-detection disabled,
  - Google sign-in exchanges the returned authorization `code` with `exchangeCodeForSession()` instead of accepting access/refresh tokens from the redirect fragment,
  - cancelled browser sessions, OAuth redirect errors, and missing-code redirects now throw user-readable errors instead of silently returning,
  - Google PKCE guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed analysis cache prewarm misses:
  - prewarm stores only positive, schema-valid warm hits,
  - stale/missing warm entries fall through to a fresh Supabase cache check,
  - warm known-miss short-circuiting is removed,
  - cache prewarm guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed product-lookup cache-hit provenance:
  - cache hits return `cached.source || "cache"` instead of overwriting provenance with `"cache"`,
  - cache hits include `servedFromCache: true` as separate telemetry,
  - fresh lookup writes persist `image_url`, and cache hits return it,
  - product-lookup provenance guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed restored-session guest history migration retry:
  - restored `getSession()` users now retry guest history migration,
  - `INITIAL_SESSION` and `SIGNED_IN` auth events both route through a shared retry helper,
  - concurrent migration attempts are deduplicated per user and allowed to retry after completion/failure,
  - history migration guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed repeat guest-history migration:
  - sign-in now always checks anonymous guest history even when the per-user migrated flag already exists,
  - legacy guest history is merged and deduped into user-specific local history,
  - the anonymous guest key is removed only after a successful Supabase upsert,
  - upsert failure remains retryable and does not mark migration complete,
  - history migration guard now covers repeat guest-scan migration and post-upsert legacy cleanup.
- Fixed same-product history suppression:
  - history persistence now relies on the per-analysis `historySaved` flag instead of a cache-key timestamp suppression map,
  - repeated scans of the same product can create separate ledger rows,
  - duplicate writes for the same in-flight analysis are still suppressed,
  - history ledger guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed Home history "Show all" cap:
  - expanded history now renders every retained history row instead of stopping at 10,
  - collapsed history still shows the latest 3 rows,
  - "Show all" copy continues to reflect the full retained history count,
  - history UI guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Aligned local replayable result retention with retained history:
  - local full-result payload retention now keeps 50 entries to match retained history rows,
  - stale history replay copy no longer claims a hardcoded 7-day cache policy,
  - history replay miss copy now tells the user to scan again to refresh the analysis,
  - history retention guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened signed-in history sync against local storage failures:
  - completed scan history entries still attempt the signed-in Supabase upsert when AsyncStorage save fails,
  - clearing signed-in history still attempts the Supabase delete when AsyncStorage removal fails,
  - guest history remains local-only because there is no server identity to write under,
  - history sync guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed clear-history durability for signed-in users:
  - `clearHistory()` now awaits the signed-in Supabase delete instead of launching it fire-and-forget,
  - local and remote deletion failures are collected after both stores are attempted and then surfaced to the caller,
  - Home clears the visible history list only after `clearHistory()` succeeds,
  - failed clears show a visible error alert and reload history so remote rows do not silently reappear later,
  - history clear guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Removed scan-photo URI retention from history:
  - completed scan history entries no longer persist the original local camera file URI,
  - remote Supabase history rows explicitly write `photo_uri: null`, including when migrating older local entries,
  - remote history reads do not expose obsolete synced `photo_uri` values back to the UI,
  - in-app and public privacy copy now states that scan photos are not saved in scan history,
  - history photo privacy guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Tightened human-food completion schema and species handling:
  - client and edge validation now require the full safety response shape, including summary, explanation, symptoms, portions, preparation, disclaimer, and age guidance,
  - human-food analysis is stamped with the requested `petType` before validation, local state completion, and persistence,
  - non-streaming edge human-food schema failures return a retryable incomplete-response error,
  - human-food schema guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Required explicit dog/cat context for pet-food scoring:
  - pet-food analysis completion now requires `petType` to be `dog` or `cat` before local state, cache, or history persistence,
  - search, front-photo, and ingredient-label recovery flows pause with a dog/cat confirmation UI when species is missing or ambiguous,
  - front-photo analysis uses a selected route pet type before trusting model-detected species,
  - pet-food analysis cache and history replay keys are species-specific, while legacy speciesless cache entries are accepted only when the stored result has the same pet type,
  - pet-food species guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Removed shared cache writes for human-food safety answers:
  - `human_food` mode now exits `writeToCache()` before any `analysis_cache` upsert,
  - dog/cat human-food answers remain validated and returned to the requesting client but are not stored in the shared cross-user analysis cache,
  - human-food schema guard now verifies the no-shared-cache policy.
- Fixed expired analysis-cache cleanup:
  - added `024_fix_cleanup_expired_cache.sql` to replace `cleanup_expired_cache()`,
  - removed scalar `DELETE ... RETURNING ... INTO` row handling that can fail when multiple expired rows are deleted,
  - the replacement function deletes all expired rows, reads `ROW_COUNT`, schema-qualifies `public.analysis_cache`, pins `search_path`, and remains service-role only,
  - cache cleanup guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened paid Edge Function CORS:
  - `analyze` and `product-lookup` no longer return `Access-Control-Allow-Origin: *`,
  - browser-origin requests are allowed only when the origin is listed in `ALLOWED_CORS_ORIGINS`,
  - native app requests without an `Origin` header remain supported,
  - localhost CORS is allowed only outside `ENVIRONMENT=production`,
  - edge CORS guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened authenticated helper and product-lookup rate limits:
  - authenticated `analyze` helper modes (`identify`, `ocr_ingredients`, `ingredients_lookup`) now use a separate hourly fail-closed bucket instead of sharing the primary scan bucket or remaining loosely bounded,
  - helper product-name prompts are trimmed and capped at 200 characters before model calls,
  - authenticated `product-lookup` requests now use a dedicated hourly fail-closed bucket before ScrapingBee/OPFF work,
  - product lookup `productName` and `brand` are normalized and length-clamped before cache lookup or scraping,
  - edge quota and product-lookup security guards are included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed product-lookup service-role authentication:
  - product lookup no longer trusts an unverified decoded JWT `role` claim to bypass rate limits,
  - service-role bypass now requires the exact configured `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`,
  - user JWTs continue through `supabase.auth.getUser(token)`,
  - product-lookup security guard rejects the old decoded-payload service-role pattern.
- Hardened product-lookup match validation:
  - added a shared title/brand/species/flavor validator for positive product lookup results,
  - Amazon, Chewy, and OPFF results now return `found: false` instead of caching when the matched page/product conflicts with the requested brand, product tokens, dog/cat species, or requested flavor,
  - OPFF matching now receives the requested pet type instead of validating only by ingredient presence,
  - OPFF name search now builds candidates from all ingredient-bearing search rows, includes OPFF category/tag metadata in the shared match text, validates every candidate before returning a positive match, and no longer falls back to the first search result,
  - OPFF positive results avoid publishing an undefined-barcode source URL,
  - product lookup match guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened photo/search product-data exact-key matching:
  - exact cache-key candidates now retain confidence rank (`productName`, `brand + productName`, `brand + variant`, `productName + variant`, then broad model `searchTerms`) instead of being flattened into an unranked set,
  - exact-key rows must pass brand, significant-token, and variant agreement checks before the app treats them as catalog-backed ingredients,
  - exact-key selection now ranks by key confidence first, match score second, and ingredient count only as a tie-breaker,
  - broad AI search terms can no longer beat a canonical product row just because the neighboring row has more ingredients,
  - the manual scan-flow harness mirrors the production matcher,
  - cache exact-key guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened pet-food analysis schema validation:
  - Edge pet-food validation now requires product/pet/score, summary, verdict, ingredient rows, the full seven-category v2 rubric, nutrition analysis, processing metadata, AAFCO/completeness, recall history/severity, and testing transparency,
  - malformed pet-food non-stream responses now return a retryable 502 before quota commits, trusted OCR catalog saves, shared-cache writes, local-cache writes, or history saves,
  - streaming cache writes log and skip pet-food schema rejects instead of treating skeletal results as valid completions,
  - pre-call shared analysis-cache hits now require both current `schemaVersion` and schema-valid analysis shape before being served,
  - client streaming and non-streaming parsers reject incomplete pet-food results before final `onUpdate`,
  - analysis-service local result/history/completion gates use the same rich pet-food validator,
  - pet-food schema guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Cleaned catalog display text quality:
  - added `026_cleanup_product_display_text.sql` to decode common HTML entities in `product_data.product_name` and `product_data.brand`,
  - the migration strips scraped `Brand:`/`Product:` prefixes and collapses whitespace without changing cache keys,
  - product lookup now sanitizes scraped product/brand display values before writing `product_data` rows or returning lookup responses,
  - catalog cleanup guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Moved Supabase auth-session persistence to native secure storage:
  - added `expo-secure-store` and the Expo config plugin,
  - Supabase auth now uses a `nativeSecureAuthStorage` adapter instead of direct AsyncStorage,
  - native reads migrate legacy Supabase auth sessions from AsyncStorage into SecureStore and remove the old AsyncStorage value,
  - native SecureStore write failures do not fall back to insecure AsyncStorage persistence,
  - AsyncStorage remains only as a web fallback for auth storage,
  - auth storage guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed in-app legal/privacy mismatches:
  - Terms no longer claim Apple/Google sign-in is required to use the app while guest scanning exists,
  - Privacy now discloses guest usage information and local guest history behavior,
  - Privacy now discloses both Anthropic Claude and OpenAI model use for analysis, product identification, OCR, and ingredient lookup,
  - Privacy now discloses server-side public product lookup through ScrapingBee/public product websites,
  - retention copy now distinguishes guest local history, signed-in history, cached product analyses, and account deletion,
  - security copy now mentions native secure storage for auth sessions where supported,
  - subscription terms no longer imply every plan has a free trial,
  - legal copy guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Added first-use legal consent gating:
  - scan, search-result analysis, typed human-food safety checks, and human-food camera checks now require a dated Terms/Privacy acceptance before starting the action,
  - acceptance is persisted under a versioned June 8, 2026 key so future legal updates can require a new acceptance,
  - Terms and Privacy can be read inside the consent modal before accepting,
  - human-food entry now checks the dedicated human-food quota instead of the pet-food scan quota before opening the safety modal,
  - legal consent guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened legal/support WebViews:
  - local in-app Terms/Privacy HTML WebViews now disable JavaScript and DOM storage,
  - local HTML WebViews are restricted to `about:blank` origins and multiple windows are disabled,
  - the shared WebView screen restricts external URL loads to HTTPS origins,
  - WebView security guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Hardened production device logging:
  - added a production-only startup log filter that suppresses `console.log`, `console.info`, and `console.debug` in release builds,
  - development builds keep debug logging,
  - `console.warn` and `console.error` remain available for release diagnostics,
  - production log guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed public website/support/legal mismatches:
  - public App Store link now uses the canonical App Store Connect ID `6760733899`,
  - public support copy now describes the current front-package-first scan flow and ingredient-panel fallback,
  - public support subscription cancellation copy covers both iOS and Android,
  - public Privacy date/footer are current and match the in-app June 8, 2026 legal update,
  - public Privacy now discloses guest usage, local guest history, OpenAI, Anthropic, Open Pet Food Facts, ScrapingBee/public product lookup, cached analysis retention, and native secure auth storage,
  - public Terms no longer claim sign-in is required,
  - public Terms no longer hardcode stale weekly/monthly/annual prices or imply every plan has a 3-day trial,
  - public docs guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Reduced abandoned-scan quota/accounting exposure:
  - `analysisService.cancelAnalysis()` now aborts a running analysis that no mounted Results subscriber owns,
  - Results cancels unfinished running analyses when the screen is unfocused and unmounted,
  - ingredient-photo recovery now marks the analysis entry as `needs_ingredient_photo` instead of leaving it `running`,
  - analysis completion guard covers abandoned-analysis cancellation and ingredient-photo pause state.
- Moved completed-analysis quota commits to the trusted Edge Function for new clients:
  - primary pet-food and human-food analyze requests now opt into `serverQuotaAccounting`,
  - helper OCR, identify, and ingredient-lookup requests do not opt into completed-scan accounting,
  - the Edge Function commits free-user quota only after a schema-valid completed result,
  - signed-in client quota increment helpers now mirror delivered quota locally for immediate UI updates without mutating server quota a second time,
  - old clients that omit the opt-in flag keep the previous post-result client RPC path during rollout,
  - server quota accounting guards are included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed recall summary RPC schema lint failure:
  - `get_brand_recall_summary()` now qualifies `brand_recalls` columns inside its aggregate query, removing the PL/pgSQL ambiguity between the returned `severity` OUT column and the table column,
  - added `025_fix_brand_recall_summary.sql` so already-migrated databases receive the corrected function definition,
  - updated the original `016_brand_recalls.sql` definition so fresh local rebuilds install the corrected function,
  - recall RPC guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed signed-in human-food history replay:
  - `scan_history` now has user-scoped `safety_level` and `analysis_payload` columns for human-food entries, with a safety-level check constraint,
  - completed human-food history entries persist the validated safety payload locally and to Supabase without reintroducing shared `analysis_cache` writes,
  - Home passes the stored human-food history payload into Results, and Results renders that payload before falling back to local/shared cache lookup,
  - privacy copy now explicitly discloses account-synced human-food safety details in scan history,
  - human-food history replay guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed human-food caution explanation copy:
  - explanation headings now map all three safety states explicitly,
  - `safe` renders "Why It's Likely Safe",
  - `caution` renders "Why To Use Caution" instead of being collapsed into dangerous copy,
  - `dangerous` remains "Why It's Dangerous",
  - human-food safety copy guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Improved veterinary disclaimer visibility at decision points:
  - Home's human-food entry card now labels the feature as an AI estimate, not veterinary advice,
  - the human-food submit modal shows a vet/pet-poison-control caveat before text or photo submission,
  - onboarding safety examples now include informational-use and ingestion-concern caveats,
  - Paywall copy now markets "Human food safety estimates" instead of an unconditional checker,
  - completed pet-food results show the AI/veterinary disclaimer for all users, not only Pro users,
  - completed human-food results show the disclaimer near the safety verdict instead of only after all detail sections,
  - veterinary disclaimer guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Preserved ingredient-source provenance through analysis:
  - product-data sources are classified as authoritative, listing-derived, community/OCR, scraped, or unknown,
  - search, photo DB-hit, shared-cache, local-cache, and label-OCR recovery paths stamp completed analyses with source trust metadata instead of forcing `ingredientSource = "verified"`,
  - current `product_data.source` overrides stale `analysis_cache.data_source = "verified"` when replaying cached analyses,
  - Home search result pills distinguish verified, listing, retailer, and label-photo sources,
  - Results shows a lower-provenance ingredient notice for listing/scraped/user-OCR/catalog-derived rows,
  - onboarding catalog copy now says indexed recipes with source labels instead of claiming every recipe is verified,
  - the Edge Function prompt now describes source-labeled ingredient data and tells the model not to call listing/scraped/user-OCR data verified unless the source trust is authoritative,
  - `analysis_cache.data_source` now preserves the verified-mode source from `opffProduct.source`,
  - ingredient provenance guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Fixed shared analysis-cache lookup-type metadata:
  - `analyzeWithData()` now forwards an explicit `lookupType` to the Edge Function,
  - barcode analysis sends `lookupType: "barcode"`,
  - search, photo DB-hit, and label-photo verified-analysis paths send `lookupType: "name"` even when they use a shared product cache key,
  - the Edge cache writer prefers explicit `lookupType` and only falls back to barcode-shaped numeric keys for older clients,
  - added `028_fix_analysis_cache_lookup_type.sql` to delete obsolete human-food cache rows and backfill existing cache rows to barcode/name by key shape,
  - cache lookup-type guard is included in `npm run test:guards`.
- Bounded AI auth-header acquisition:
  - `_getAuthHeaders()` now races Supabase `getSession()` and token refresh work against a 4-second auth budget in addition to the caller's request abort signal,
  - slow auth lookup/refresh now raises a typed `AUTH_SESSION_UNKNOWN` retryable error instead of silently waiting outside the user-visible scan budget,
  - signed-in refresh/token failures still fail closed with `AUTH_SESSION_EXPIRED` instead of downgrading to guest headers,
  - identify, OCR, product lookup, streaming analysis, and non-streaming analysis keep their operation timers wrapped around auth-header acquisition,
  - scanner mount `checkSession()` now bounds proactive session read/refresh work to 4 seconds and remains non-blocking,
  - Claude timeout and auth-session guards cover bounded auth-header and scanner pre-refresh behavior.
- Verified and strengthened guest quota reconciliation hardening:
  - malformed, negative, and oversized local quota mirrors are parsed through `parseStoredQuotaCount(...)` before any UI or sign-in carryover use,
  - pet-food guest-to-account carryover is bounded by `FREE_SCAN_LIMIT` and cannot replay a corrupted `@woof_scan_count` value into unbounded server RPCs,
  - human-food guest-to-account carryover is clamped to the daily free limit and limited to at most one server increment,
  - signed-in delivered-quota mirrors remain local/UI-only because completed quota commits are owned by the Edge Function,
  - auth quota guard now asserts the exact bounded carryover invariants for corrupted local scan and human-food counts.
- Verified history replay retention hardening:
  - retained local replayable result payloads now match the retained scan-history row count (`50`),
  - stale-schema local payloads and stale shared analysis-cache rows are treated as misses instead of rendering old scoring models,
  - history replay miss copy no longer claims a hardcoded 7-day cache policy,
  - history replay misses show a clear expired-result message and route the CTA back to the scan/home flow instead of retrying a known-missing cache entry,
  - focused history guards cover retention alignment, expanded history rendering, ledger behavior, sync durability, and Results error routing.
- Verified first-scan education toast rendering:
  - `FirstScanToast` is mounted in the Results success layout,
  - `@woof_first_scan_toast_shown` is written only after the toast becomes visible,
  - Results guard covers the toast mount point, delayed persistence, and overlay positioning.
- Verified search catalog-miss recovery:
  - catalog misses classify as `product_not_found` with `action: "scan_product"`,
  - Results error state routes the primary CTA to scanner/product capture instead of remounting the same failed search route,
  - rejected search cache keys are removed from recent searches and Home rehydrates recents on focus,
  - focused search recovery, Results error, and Home search guards cover the loop prevention.

  - this closes a remaining infinite-loading path where search or identified-product flows could emit `need_pet_type` before Results had assigned the service key used to match events.

  - analysis flows pass their controller signal into those reads, so Results unmounts, cancellation, or hard analysis timeouts abort pending database work instead of waiting in the background,
  - catalog lookup timeouts now surface as retryable database-check errors rather than falling through to product-not-found or ingredient-label capture flows.

  - the Edge Function now uses a shared request-linked Supabase deadline helper for pre-call cache reads, brand-profile enrichment, cache writes, trusted user-OCR catalog writes, and completed quota commits,

- Hardened analysis cleanup timers against retry/replay races:
  - cleanup timers now clear any previous timer for the canonical key and capture the exact analysis state that scheduled cleanup,
  - delayed cleanup only deletes the entry if the current in-memory entry is still that same terminal state, so old error/cancelled/not-found cleanup cannot delete a fresh retry result under the same product key,
  - rekeying and new analysis startup clear stale cleanup timers before reusing a key, preventing old terminal or paused recovery state from orphaning newer Results replay.

  - OPFF lookups now use a shared request helper that links the local 4-second OPFF deadline to the caller's analysis abort signal,
  - barcode analysis passes its controller signal into `lookupBarcode()`, so Results unmounts, retries, and hard analysis timeouts stop the OPFF fetch/body read instead of waiting for the isolated OPFF timer,
  - parent abort listeners are removed during request cleanup, and caller-aborted OPFF requests return an aborted miss without reporting a network failure.

  - `npm run backfill:catalog -- --dry-run` reads existing curated product lists, skips existing `product_data.cache_key` rows, and reports missing candidates without touching data,
  - real runs require `PRODUCT_LOOKUP_SERVICE_KEY`, `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, or `SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY` by default, so broad imports do not fall back to anonymous product-lookup limits or reopen client-side catalog writes,
  - dry-run on June 12, 2026 found 387 curated candidates, 9,233 existing keys, and 384 missing curated targets; this helps but is not enough to reach 12k by itself,
  - broad OPFF API probes were unreliable (`500`/`504` on broad category endpoints), and the responding narrow endpoints yielded only ~51 mostly non-US missing candidates, so OPFF cannot close the current US catalog gap alone.
- `supabase db push`, `supabase migration list`, production REST probes for `log_product_event`, `scan_history.analysis_payload`, and `product_data`, `node --check scripts/backfill-product-catalog-via-lookup.js`, `node --check scripts/test-catalog-backfill-guards.js`, `npm run test:catalog-backfill`, `npm run backfill:catalog -- --dry-run --limit=25`, `node --check scripts/audit-product-catalog.js`, `npm run test:product-catalog-audit`, `npm run audit:catalog -- --json`, `npm run test:guards`, `npm run check:config`, `npm run check:edge`, and `npm audit --audit-level=moderate` passed after the cloud migration/backfill/audit work. `npm run check:catalog` correctly remains failing because rows are 9,233 < 12,000, analysis-ready rows are 9,233 < 10,000, and fresh analysis-cache rows are 0 < 8,000.
- Added service-key-aware analysis cache precompute tooling:
  - `npm run precompute:analysis -- --dry-run --limit=25` reads the live clean `product_data` catalog, skips only service-key-verified fresh schema-valid `analysis_cache` entries, and reports selected precompute rows without calling `analyze`,
  - real runs require `ANALYZE_SERVICE_KEY`, `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, or `SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY` by default, so broad score precomputes do not consume anonymous/user scan quota,
  - analyze calls use verified mode with `stream: false`, `lookupType: "name"`, and `serverQuotaAccounting: false`, passing the cleaned ingredient list, source provenance, image URL, and any nutrient panel through the existing Edge scoring path,
  - dry-run on June 12, 2026 reported 9,233 analysis-ready product rows, cache coverage unverified without `ANALYZE_SERVICE_KEY` / `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, 9,233 eligible precompute rows, and 10 selected with `--limit=10`.
- Deployed validated Edge Functions to production after local `npm run check:edge` passed:
  - `analyze` advanced from version 61 / 2026-04-23 to version 62 / 2026-06-12 22:15:45 UTC,
  - `product-lookup` advanced from version 46 / 2026-04-19 to version 47 / 2026-06-12 22:15:51 UTC,
  - a production `product-lookup` smoke test returned HTTP 200 from `product_data` cache with `found: true`, `servedFromCache: true`, and a 19-ingredient payload.
- Hardened the product display-text contract again after the production smoke test exposed punctuation artifacts that the first audit did not count:
  - added migration `038_harden_product_display_punctuation.sql` to extend `clean_product_display_text()` for numeric HTML entities, leading/trailing pipe characters, dangling opening parentheses, and trailing punctuation,
  - extended `npm run audit:catalog` dirty-display detection so these scraped display artifacts fail the strict release gate,
  - pushed migration `038` to the cloud; `supabase migration list` now shows local and remote aligned through `038`,
  - production catalog audit after migration `038` reports 9,233 total rows, 9,233 analysis-ready rows, 0 short-ingredient rows, 0 dirty display rows, 0 expired rows, and 9,166 image rows.
- Hardened catalog/cache verification after confirming local env has no service-role/analyze/product-lookup/ScrapingBee/model keys available:
  - `npm run audit:catalog` now accepts `PRODUCT_CATALOG_SERVICE_KEY`, `ANALYSIS_CACHE_AUDIT_KEY`, `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, or `SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY` for service-key analysis-cache coverage counts,
  - strict `npm run check:catalog` now fails when analysis-cache coverage is not service-key verified, instead of treating anon-visible cache rows as authoritative,
  - `npm run precompute:analysis -- --dry-run` now reports cache coverage as unverified when no service/analyze key is present, instead of implying a proven zero-cache state,
  - `.env.example` now documents the offline-only service-key variables needed for catalog import, cache precompute, and service-key-verified catalog audits.
- `node --check scripts/precompute-analysis-cache.js`, `node --check scripts/test-analysis-precompute-guards.js`, `npm run test:analysis-precompute`, `npm run precompute:analysis -- --dry-run --limit=10`, `node --check scripts/audit-product-catalog.js`, `npm run test:product-catalog-audit`, `npm run audit:catalog -- --json`, `npm run test:guards`, `npm run check:config`, `npm run check:edge`, and `npm audit --audit-level=moderate` passed after the cache-verification hardening. `npm run check:catalog` was also run and correctly fails because rows are 9,233 < 12,000, analysis-ready rows are 9,233 < 10,000, the anon-visible fresh analysis-cache count is 0 < 8,000, and cache coverage is not service-key verified in the current local environment.
- Hardened production-scale analysis precompute execution:
  - `npm run precompute:analysis` now verifies each successful `analyze` call by reading the target `analysis_cache` row back with the service/analyze key and requiring the current schema-valid analysis shape,
  - write verification is enabled by default when a service key is present, can be explicitly disabled with `--no-verify-writes`, and reports `verified cached`, `accepted`, `unverified`, and `failed` counts separately,
  - `--max-failures=N` stops long runs after repeated failed or unverified writes, and the script exits nonzero if any production write could not be verified,
  - `--verify-delay-ms=N` controls retry pacing for cache-write verification so asynchronous cache writes have time to appear before being counted as unverified.
- `node --check scripts/precompute-analysis-cache.js`, `node --check scripts/test-analysis-precompute-guards.js`, `npm run test:analysis-precompute`, `npm run precompute:analysis -- --dry-run --limit=10`, `npm run test:guards`, `npm run check:config`, `npm run check:edge`, `npm audit --audit-level=moderate`, and `npm run audit:catalog -- --json` passed after precompute write-verification hardening.
- Added resumable precompute reporting:
  - `npm run precompute:analysis` now supports `--report=path.jsonl` to append redacted per-row JSONL entries for `precompute_start`, `precompute_result`, and `precompute_done`,
  - `--resume-report` reads the same report and skips only rows with prior `verified_cached` entries, so failed/unverified attempts are retried rather than hidden,
  - report entries include cache key, source, pet type, ingredient count, HTTP status, and verification reason, but not raw ingredient text or model output,
  - dry-run with `--report=.tmp/precompute-report.jsonl --resume-report` confirmed the live selection still reports 9,233 analysis-ready rows, 0 report-verified skips, 9,233 eligible rows, and 10 selected without writing the report.

- Hardened production-scale catalog backfill execution:
  - `npm run backfill:catalog` now verifies successful `product-lookup` responses by reading the target `product_data.cache_key` back and requiring an analysis-ready ingredient count,
  - write verification is enabled by default, can be disabled with `--no-verify-writes`, and reports `verified saved`, `accepted`, `unverified`, `not found`, and `failed` counts separately,
  - `--max-failures=N` stops long catalog-fill runs after repeated failed or unverified writes, and the script exits nonzero if any import failed or could not be verified,
  - `--report=path.jsonl` appends redacted per-target JSONL entries for `catalog_backfill_start`, `catalog_backfill_result`, and `catalog_backfill_done`,
  - `--resume-report` reads the same report and skips only prior `verified_saved` cache keys, so not-found/failed/unverified targets can be retried after scraper or source improvements,
  - dry-run with `--report=.tmp/catalog-backfill-report.jsonl --resume-report` confirmed 387 curated candidates, 9,233 existing cache keys, 0 report-verified skips, 384 missing curated targets, and 10 selected without writing the report.

- Shortened the app-level analysis hard timeout to match the request-layer deadlines:
  - `ANALYSIS_TIMEOUT_MS` is now 70s, slightly above the longest Claude client request deadline of 60s, instead of 120s,
  - this prevents Results from sitting in a loading state for another minute after the underlying scan/verified-analysis request has already timed out,
  - the analysis-completion guard now enforces that the hard timeout stays near the request deadline.

- Removed a duplicate selected-search catalog round trip:
  - Home now passes a compact `catalogSnapshot` from the final post-consent `getProductDataByCacheKey(...)` validation into Results,
  - Results forwards the snapshot to `analysisService.startAnalysis(...)` for search mode,
  - `analysisService` accepts the snapshot only when its `productCacheKey` exactly matches the selected search cache key and it still has at least 5 clean ingredients,
  - malformed, wrong-key, or incomplete snapshots fall back to the existing exact Supabase `product_data` lookup, preserving stale-row/network-error behavior,
  - selected search-result taps can now proceed directly to shared analysis-cache/local-cache checks and AI scoring from the already-validated catalog row instead of fetching the same row a third time.

- Added a bounded barcode-to-catalog cache bridge:
  - after OPFF identifies a barcode product and species is known, barcode scans now make a short 1.8s max catalog/name lookup to find the matching clean `product_data` row,
  - when that row has a species-specific shared `analysis_cache` or local result, barcode scans reuse the existing catalog score instead of spending AI/quota on a new barcode-specific analysis,
  - reused catalog scores are augmented with the current catalog ingredient text/provenance and saved locally under the barcode key, so the next same-barcode scan is instant,
  - if the catalog row is found but has no cached score yet, the first barcode AI score now uses the cleaner catalog ingredient text, nutrient panel, source trust metadata, source URL, and image instead of falling back to the weaker OPFF barcode payload,
  - if the short catalog bridge misses or times out, the existing barcode-specific AI analysis path remains unchanged and still writes with `lookupType: "barcode"`.

- Added shared cache aliases for catalog-backed first-time barcode scores:
  - barcode scans still write their primary `analysis_cache` row under the barcode key with `lookupType: "barcode"`,
  - when the barcode scoring payload comes from a clean catalog row, the client also sends the catalog species cache key as a cache alias,
  - the Edge `analyze` function validates aliases before writing them: max 3 aliases, skip the primary key, max 180 characters, normalized key shape only, and dog/cat suffix must match the completed analysis species,
  - validated alias rows are written with `lookup_type: "name"` and the same normalized analysis/provenance, so later search/photo/catalog paths can reuse a barcode-first score without another AI call,
  - human-food analysis still bypasses shared cache writes before alias handling.

- Tightened product-data lookup budgets:
  - `getProductData(..., { timeoutMs })` now treats `timeoutMs` as a total lookup budget across exact-key candidates and scored fallback search,
  - short callers such as the 1.8s barcode catalog bridge can no longer spend the full timeout on the exact query and then wait through a second full scored fallback timeout,
  - normal search/photo lookups keep the existing 8s default budget, but the fallback query only receives whatever time remains after exact-key matching,
  - budget exhaustion returns a `lookup_error` instead of silently converting a slow database/network path into a false product-not-found result.

  - `_getSpeciesCachedAnalysis()` now batches species-specific candidates and then legacy speciesless candidates instead of performing one Supabase request per candidate key,
  - priority order is preserved by reading the returned hit map in the existing candidate order, so shared catalog keys still win over fallback product-name keys,
  - batch hits still record non-blocking cache-hit telemetry and are linked to the analysis abort signal, so unmounted/retried scans do not continue abandoned cache work.

- Hardened runtime handling for stale Supabase schema-cache errors seen during real scans:
  - analytics now treats PostgREST `PGRST202` as an unavailable `log_product_event` RPC and suppresses non-critical event writes during the retry window, even when the returned message shape differs from the text-only "schema cache" error,
  - history sync now treats PostgREST `PGRST204` as a missing optional `scan_history` column error,
  - `product_image_url` is now part of the optional remote history-column fallback, so an older history schema can still sync the core scan row instead of failing the whole upsert because an image URL column is unavailable,
  - rich human-food replay fields (`safety_level`, `analysis_payload`) remain protected from lossy remote fallback; if those columns are unavailable and the entry contains rich replay data, the full entry stays local and remote migration/upsert defers until the schema is available.

- Added and deployed a server-owned RevenueCat entitlement sync path for the "client says Pro but analyze enforces free quota" failure mode:
  - new `supabase/functions/revenuecat-webhook` verifies RevenueCat's `Authorization: Bearer <REVENUECAT_WEBHOOK_AUTH_TOKEN>` header before doing any work,
  - for each Supabase UUID App User ID in the webhook payload, it calls RevenueCat's server REST `/v1/subscribers/{app_user_id}` endpoint using `REVENUECAT_REST_API_KEY`, reads the current `pro` entitlement, and updates only server-owned `profiles.is_pro`, `profiles.pro_expires_at`, and `profiles.updated_at` with the Supabase service role,
  - it ignores RevenueCat dashboard `TEST` events and non-Supabase/anonymous app user IDs, and handles transfer ID arrays by syncing every UUID candidate from RevenueCat's current subscriber state instead of trusting raw event ordering,
  - `npm run check:edge` now type-checks the webhook with the other Edge Functions, and `npm run test:revenuecat-webhook` is part of `npm run test:guards`,
  - `.env.example` and `docs/release-verification.md` now document the required webhook/API secrets plus sandbox verification against `profiles.is_pro`.
- Pre-change guards `npm run test:server-quota-accounting`, `npm run test:edge-quota`, `npm run test:claude-auth-session`, and `npm run test:purchase-entitlement` passed before this edit. Local environment inspection still shows `REVENUECAT_WEBHOOK_AUTH_TOKEN`, `REVENUECAT_REST_API_KEY`, and `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` missing, so production still needs Supabase Edge Function secrets set and the RevenueCat dashboard webhook configured before this path can update Pro quota state.
- Opened shared pet-food analysis-cache reads to the app's guest path:

  - `increment_cache_hit(TEXT)` is now a bounded `SECURITY DEFINER` function with `search_path = public`, so guest and signed-in cache hits can update telemetry without direct table update privileges or noisy RLS failures,

- Added and deployed on-demand RevenueCat entitlement recovery inside `analyze`:
  - when a signed-in user's `profiles.is_pro` is false and the request is about to be blocked by the free pet-food or human-food quota, `analyze` now performs a bounded server-side RevenueCat `/v1/subscribers/{supabase_user_id}` lookup using `REVENUECAT_REST_API_KEY`,
  - if RevenueCat's current subscriber state has an active `pro` entitlement, `analyze` updates `profiles.is_pro = true` and `pro_expires_at`, then lets the scan continue instead of returning "Free scan limit reached",
  - if the server API key is missing, RevenueCat is unavailable, or the entitlement is inactive, the existing fail-closed quota response remains unchanged,
  - the recovery path is linked to the client request signal, has a 5s timeout, emits redacted `revenuecat_entitlement_recovery` audit markers, and does not trust client-provided Pro state.

- Abort-propagated Home history loads:

  - `services/history.js` now threads the parent abort signal through auth session lookup, Supabase `scan_history` reads, and product image enrichment reads, while keeping existing internal 3s/5s/2.5s deadlines and suppressing expected abort noise,
  - this stops superseded/timed-out history loads from continuing remote work after Home has moved on to a newer load.

- Corrected analyze network health reporting:
  - `services/claude.js` now reports streaming analyze success only after the Edge response is HTTP OK,
  - streaming HTTP failures are reported through the nonblocking network detector before throwing, and bounded non-streaming analyze fallbacks report network/timeout failures before returning typed timeout errors,
  - this keeps the app's offline/online state aligned with real analyze availability instead of clearing recent network failures on quota/server responses.

  - `scripts/test-analysis-precompute-guards.js` now preserves both the indexed planning query and the fatal analyze response handling.

This should make search-result taps load scores faster after migration deployment because Results can skip the extra exact `product_data` round trip and immediately race local/shared analysis-cache replay or model scoring from the supplied verified ingredients.

- Hardened client behavior for the Supabase schema-cache mismatches seen in device logs:
  - `services/history.js` still protects `analysis_payload` because it is required for private human-food history replay, but no longer treats `safety_level` as unstrippable during remote history fallback, so ordinary pet-food history rows can sync to legacy `scan_history` schemas instead of repeatedly failing when `safety_level` or `analysis_payload` are absent or stale in PostgREST's schema cache,
  - local history remains the source of truth for immediate replay while reduced remote rows are attempted under bounded deadlines and inflight caps,
  - `services/analytics.js` now classifies analytics RPC schema failures using PostgREST `message`, `details`, `hint`, and `code`, so `log_product_event(...p_metadata...)` schema-cache misses are suppressed with backoff instead of surfacing as repeated runtime log noise,
  - guards now pin both the history fallback split and the broader analytics schema-error classifier.

  - `scripts/export-victor-sitemap-targets.js` reads `https://victorpetfood.com/sitemap.xml`, keeps only allowlisted official `/products/<slug>` dog/cat food URLs, derives clean product titles from those slugs, and uses anon Supabase reads only to skip existing `product_data` cache-key/name aliases,
  - the exporter keeps dog formulas from an explicit food allowlist such as Hi-Pro Plus, High Energy, Multi-Pro, Professional, Elite Canine, Yukon River Canine, Lamb Meal Sweet Potato, Ocean Fish, Beef/Lamb Brown Rice, Performance, Nutra Pro, Senior Healthy Weight, Active Dog Puppy, and Hero Canine, plus cat formulas such as Hi-Pro Plus Cat, Fit Feline, Mers Classic Feline, Mers Feline, and Grain-Free Fit Feline,
  - category rows, crunchy treats, ambiguous formulas, supplements, accessories, and non-food rows are rejected by default, and species qualifiers are preserved where needed so dog and cat formulas with similar titles do not collapse under shared lookup aliases,
  - targets are backfill-compatible official-brand slug rows and intentionally exclude raw ingredients, ingredient text, analysis payloads, OCR/base64 data, and product-page scrape payloads,
  - `package.json` exposes `npm run export:victor-sitemap-catalog`, `scripts/test-victor-sitemap-catalog-export-guards.js` is included in `npm run test:guards`, and the active short current queue remains `.tmp/catalog-backfill-current-targets.json` plus `.tmp/catalog-backfill-current-prioritized.json`.

  - `scripts/export-openfarm-nutrient-panels.js` reads the official `https://openfarmpet.com/products.json?limit=250` Shopify feed, keeps only complete dog/cat food rows, rejects treats, supplements, broths, bundles, meal-plan/gift rows, hidden/non-salable rows, and non-food rows, then fetches official Open Farm product pages for the published `Guaranteed Analysis` table,
  - the exporter normalizes as-fed protein, fat, fiber/fibre, moisture, ash, calcium, phosphorus, omega-3, omega-6, `calories_per_kg`, and `calories_per_cup` into the existing `nutrientPanel` shape, preserves the official product-page `source_url`, and emits only `cacheKey`, product identity, source metadata, and nutrient-panel fields,
  - targets are matched to existing `product_data` cache-key/name aliases before they are considered write-ready, so parsed pages without a stable catalog row stay out of the write batch instead of risking nutrient updates on the wrong product,
  - the exporter has bounded 429/503 retry/backoff and paced page requests for official-site rate limiting,
  - `package.json` exposes `npm run export:openfarm-nutrient-panels`, and `scripts/test-openfarm-nutrient-panel-export-guards.js` is included in `npm run test:guards`.

- Hardened and deployed the live search/catalog RPC after a production probe found `search_products('blue buffalo chicken')` returning a generic brand-only `blue Buffalo` row with a huge inline `data:image` payload:
  - `047_reject_brand_only_catalog_rows.sql` extends the database non-product detector to reject exact brand-only/brand-repeated rows, deletes existing matches, strips inline `data:` image URLs from existing and future `product_data` rows, and updates `search_products()` to exclude brand-only rows and null inline image payloads,
  - `048_reoptimize_search_products_snapshot.sql` adds lower-case trigram indexes and rewrites `search_products()` so it ranks and caps matching rows before unnesting ingredient arrays for sanitized catalog snapshots, preventing statement timeouts on the larger live catalog,
  - `scripts/test-search-catalog-quality-guards.js` and `scripts/test-product-display-contract-guards.js` now cover the brand-only rejection, inline image stripping, sanitized snapshot contract, and match-before-sanitize performance shape.

The current eligible refresh command is `npm run precompute:analysis -- --dry-run --demand-input='.tmp/precompute-eligible-targets.json,.tmp/catalog-backfill-report.jsonl' --report='.tmp/precompute-report.jsonl' --resume-report --export-eligible='.tmp/precompute-eligible-targets.json'`. The precompute script writes app-aligned species-specific keys (`cache_key__dog` / `cache_key__cat`) while reporting `product_cache_key` separately; current app-visible REST dry-run planning now finds 6,818 complete-food species targets from 6,181 complete-food product rows after excluding 2,988 non-complete-food rows and skipping exact species-specific, product-name, brand+product, and pet-matched legacy cache rows the app can already serve. Because the clean manifest is below the 8,000 fast-score gate, service-key catalog backfill needs to add more verified complete-food rows before precompute alone can satisfy the release target. The refreshed manifest is prioritized by existing local demand inputs and recent service-role product events when a service key is available, then common in-store brand rank, then source trust/richness, so first batches should improve likely store scans before obscure catalog rows. Increase concurrency carefully up to 8 only if Edge Function/model/API rate limits stay healthy.
- Live catalog has 0 published nutrient-panel rows against the new 500-row release gate, so scoring still cannot rely broadly on published nutrient data until the validated rows are written. Migration `040` is deployed and service-role-only; the remaining work is to load validated brand/manufacturer nutrient-panel data with `NUTRIENT_PANEL_SERVICE_KEY` or `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` set. The current validated official-source nutrient input is now `.tmp/nutrient-panel-validated-current-targets.json` with 501 unique write-ready rows (including 115 Blue Buffalo-family, 86 Royal Canin-family, 40 Open Farm, 38 Hill's-family, 32 ORIJEN-family, 28 Taste of the Wild, 21 Stella & Chewy's-family, 19 Earthborn Holistic, 17 Vital Essentials, 16 KOHA-family, 14 Primal-family, 14 Instinct, 11 The Honest Kitchen, 10 Canidae-family, 7 Nulo, 6 Solid Gold, 6 Wellness, 5 Ziwi Peak, 4 Freshpet-family, 4 Grandma Lucy's, 4 Fromm, 2 Merrick-family, and 2 NutriSource), and the next write command is `NUTRIENT_PANEL_SERVICE_KEY=... npm run backfill:nutrients -- --input=.tmp/nutrient-panel-validated-current-targets.json --export-targets=.tmp/nutrient-panel-normalized-targets.json --report=.tmp/nutrient-panel-backfill-report.jsonl --resume-report --concurrency=3`. The current no-raw-ingredients research queue remains `.tmp/nutrient-panel-targets-sanitized.json`; default readiness now reports 501/501 write-ready coverage from the validated official-source input when that file exists, while the research refresh command still writes sanitized missing-panel targets to `.tmp/nutrient-panel-targets-sanitized.json`.
- User OCR catalog ingestion is backend-owned and now emits redacted audit markers, but it still needs production log review against real label-photo scans before relying on it for catalog growth metrics.
- RevenueCat/App Store purchase, restore, entitlement, identity, webhook-to-`profiles.is_pro` sync, and on-demand analyze entitlement recovery still need real-device sandbox verification in a development/TestFlight/App Store build; Expo Go is not sufficient for `react-native-purchases`. The app now triggers server-side entitlement recovery earlier when the local device says Pro, but the deployed `revenuecat-webhook` and `analyze` recovery path still need `REVENUECAT_REST_API_KEY` set as a Supabase secret; the webhook also needs `REVENUECAT_WEBHOOK_AUTH_TOKEN` set and the RevenueCat dashboard webhook URL/header configured.
